            SELECT
                c.conname,
                array(
                    SELECT attname
                    FROM (
                        SELECT unnest(c.conkey) AS colid,
                               generate_series(1, array_length(c.conkey, 1)) AS arridx
                    ) AS cols
                    JOIN pg_attribute AS ca ON cols.colid = ca.attnum
                    WHERE ca.attrelid = c.conrelid
                    ORDER BY cols.arridx
                ),
                c.contype,
                (SELECT fkc.relname || '.' || fka.attname
                FROM pg_attribute AS fka
                JOIN pg_class AS fkc ON fka.attrelid = fkc.oid
                WHERE fka.attrelid = c.confrelid AND fka.attnum = c.confkey[1]),
                cl.reloptions
            FROM pg_constraint AS c
            JOIN pg_class AS cl ON c.conrelid = cl.oid
            JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON cl.relnamespace = ns.oid
            WHERE ns.nspname = 'public' AND cl.relname = 'oauth2_provider_application'
        ; args=['public', 'oauth2_provider_application']
[2017-12-13 23:34:40] DEBUG [django.db.backends:111] (0.121) 
            SELECT
                indexname, array_agg(attname ORDER BY rnum), indisunique, indisprimary,
                array_agg(ordering ORDER BY rnum), amname, exprdef, s2.attoptions
            FROM (
                SELECT
                    row_number() OVER () as rnum, c2.relname as indexname,
                    idx.*, attr.attname, am.amname,
                    CASE
                        WHEN idx.indexprs IS NOT NULL THEN
                            pg_get_indexdef(idx.indexrelid)
                    END AS exprdef,
                    CASE am.amname
                        WHEN 'btree' THEN
                            CASE (option & 1)
                                WHEN 1 THEN 'DESC' ELSE 'ASC'
                            END
                    END as ordering,
                    c2.reloptions as attoptions
                FROM (
                    SELECT
                        *, unnest(i.indkey) as key, unnest(i.indoption) as option
                    FROM pg_index i
                ) idx
                LEFT JOIN pg_class c ON idx.indrelid = c.oid
                LEFT JOIN pg_class c2 ON idx.indexrelid = c2.oid
                LEFT JOIN pg_am am ON c2.relam = am.oid
                LEFT JOIN pg_attribute attr ON attr.attrelid = c.oid AND attr.attnum = idx.key
                WHERE c.relname = 'oauth2_provider_application'
            ) s2
            GROUP BY indexname, indisunique, indisprimary, amname, exprdef, attoptions;
        ; args=['oauth2_provider_application']

            SELECT
                c.conname,
                array(
                    SELECT attname
                    FROM (
                        SELECT unnest(c.conkey) AS colid,
                               generate_series(1, array_length(c.conkey, 1)) AS arridx
                    ) AS cols
                    JOIN pg_attribute AS ca ON cols.colid = ca.attnum
                    WHERE ca.attrelid = c.conrelid
                    ORDER BY cols.arridx
                ),
                c.contype,
                (SELECT fkc.relname || '.' || fka.attname
                FROM pg_attribute AS fka
                JOIN pg_class AS fkc ON fka.attrelid = fkc.oid
                WHERE fka.attrelid = c.confrelid AND fka.attnum = c.confkey[1]),
                cl.reloptions
            FROM pg_constraint AS c
            JOIN pg_class AS cl ON c.conrelid = cl.oid
            JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON cl.relnamespace = ns.oid
            WHERE ns.nspname = 'public' AND cl.relname = 'oauth2_provider_accesstoken'

[2017-12-13 23:34:43] DEBUG [django.db.backends:111] (0.119) 
            SELECT
                indexname, array_agg(attname ORDER BY rnum), indisunique, indisprimary,
                array_agg(ordering ORDER BY rnum), amname, exprdef, s2.attoptions
            FROM (
                SELECT
                    row_number() OVER () as rnum, c2.relname as indexname,
                    idx.*, attr.attname, am.amname,
                    CASE
                        WHEN idx.indexprs IS NOT NULL THEN
                            pg_get_indexdef(idx.indexrelid)
                    END AS exprdef,
                    CASE am.amname
                        WHEN 'btree' THEN
                            CASE (option & 1)
                                WHEN 1 THEN 'DESC' ELSE 'ASC'
                            END
                    END as ordering,
                    c2.reloptions as attoptions
                FROM (
                    SELECT
                        *, unnest(i.indkey) as key, unnest(i.indoption) as option
                    FROM pg_index i
                ) idx
                LEFT JOIN pg_class c ON idx.indrelid = c.oid
                LEFT JOIN pg_class c2 ON idx.indexrelid = c2.oid
                LEFT JOIN pg_am am ON c2.relam = am.oid
                LEFT JOIN pg_attribute attr ON attr.attrelid = c.oid AND attr.attnum = idx.key
                WHERE c.relname = 'oauth2_provider_accesstoken'
            ) s2
            GROUP BY indexname, indisunique, indisprimary, amname, exprdef, attoptions;
        ; args=['oauth2_provider_accesstoken']

[2017-12-13 23:34:48] DEBUG [django.db.backends:111] (0.118) 
            SELECT
                c.conname,
                array(
                    SELECT attname
                    FROM (
                        SELECT unnest(c.conkey) AS colid,
                               generate_series(1, array_length(c.conkey, 1)) AS arridx
                    ) AS cols
                    JOIN pg_attribute AS ca ON cols.colid = ca.attnum
                    WHERE ca.attrelid = c.conrelid
                    ORDER BY cols.arridx
                ),
                c.contype,
                (SELECT fkc.relname || '.' || fka.attname
                FROM pg_attribute AS fka
                JOIN pg_class AS fkc ON fka.attrelid = fkc.oid
                WHERE fka.attrelid = c.confrelid AND fka.attnum = c.confkey[1]),
                cl.reloptions
            FROM pg_constraint AS c
            JOIN pg_class AS cl ON c.conrelid = cl.oid
            JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON cl.relnamespace = ns.oid
            WHERE ns.nspname = 'public' AND cl.relname = 'oauth2_provider_accesstoken'
        ; args=['public', 'oauth2_provider_accesstoken']
[2017-12-13 23:34:48] DEBUG [django.db.backends:111] (0.117) 
            SELECT
                indexname, array_agg(attname ORDER BY rnum), indisunique, indisprimary,
                array_agg(ordering ORDER BY rnum), amname, exprdef, s2.attoptions
            FROM (
                SELECT
                    row_number() OVER () as rnum, c2.relname as indexname,
                    idx.*, attr.attname, am.amname,
                    CASE
                        WHEN idx.indexprs IS NOT NULL THEN
                            pg_get_indexdef(idx.indexrelid)
                    END AS exprdef,
                    CASE am.amname
                        WHEN 'btree' THEN
                            CASE (option & 1)
                                WHEN 1 THEN 'DESC' ELSE 'ASC'
                            END
                    END as ordering,
                    c2.reloptions as attoptions
                FROM (
                    SELECT
                        *, unnest(i.indkey) as key, unnest(i.indoption) as option
                    FROM pg_index i
                ) idx
                LEFT JOIN pg_class c ON idx.indrelid = c.oid
                LEFT JOIN pg_class c2 ON idx.indexrelid = c2.oid
                LEFT JOIN pg_am am ON c2.relam = am.oid
                LEFT JOIN pg_attribute attr ON attr.attrelid = c.oid AND attr.attnum = idx.key
                WHERE c.relname = 'oauth2_provider_accesstoken'
            ) s2
            GROUP BY indexname, indisunique, indisprimary, amname, exprdef, attoptions;
        ; args=['oauth2_provider_accesstoken']

[2017-12-13 23:34:53] DEBUG [django.db.backends:111] (0.116) 
            SELECT
                c.conname,
                array(
                    SELECT attname
                    FROM (
                        SELECT unnest(c.conkey) AS colid,
                               generate_series(1, array_length(c.conkey, 1)) AS arridx
                    ) AS cols
                    JOIN pg_attribute AS ca ON cols.colid = ca.attnum
                    WHERE ca.attrelid = c.conrelid
                    ORDER BY cols.arridx
                ),
                c.contype,
                (SELECT fkc.relname || '.' || fka.attname
                FROM pg_attribute AS fka
                JOIN pg_class AS fkc ON fka.attrelid = fkc.oid
                WHERE fka.attrelid = c.confrelid AND fka.attnum = c.confkey[1]),
                cl.reloptions
            FROM pg_constraint AS c
            JOIN pg_class AS cl ON c.conrelid = cl.oid
            JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON cl.relnamespace = ns.oid
            WHERE ns.nspname = 'public' AND cl.relname = 'oauth2_provider_refreshtoken'
        ; args=['public', 'oauth2_provider_refreshtoken']
[2017-12-13 23:34:53] DEBUG [django.db.backends:111] (0.117) 
            SELECT
                indexname, array_agg(attname ORDER BY rnum), indisunique, indisprimary,
                array_agg(ordering ORDER BY rnum), amname, exprdef, s2.attoptions
            FROM (
                SELECT
                    row_number() OVER () as rnum, c2.relname as indexname,
                    idx.*, attr.attname, am.amname,
                    CASE
                        WHEN idx.indexprs IS NOT NULL THEN
                            pg_get_indexdef(idx.indexrelid)
                    END AS exprdef,
                    CASE am.amname
                        WHEN 'btree' THEN
                            CASE (option & 1)
                                WHEN 1 THEN 'DESC' ELSE 'ASC'
                            END
                    END as ordering,
                    c2.reloptions as attoptions
                FROM (
                    SELECT
                        *, unnest(i.indkey) as key, unnest(i.indoption) as option
                    FROM pg_index i
                ) idx
                LEFT JOIN pg_class c ON idx.indrelid = c.oid
                LEFT JOIN pg_class c2 ON idx.indexrelid = c2.oid
                LEFT JOIN pg_am am ON c2.relam = am.oid
                LEFT JOIN pg_attribute attr ON attr.attrelid = c.oid AND attr.attnum = idx.key
                WHERE c.relname = 'oauth2_provider_refreshtoken'
            ) s2
            GROUP BY indexname, indisunique, indisprimary, amname, exprdef, attoptions;
        ; args=['oauth2_provider_refreshtoken']

[2017-12-13 23:35:00] DEBUG [django.db.backends:111] (0.239) 
            SELECT
                c.conname,
                array(
                    SELECT attname
                    FROM (
                        SELECT unnest(c.conkey) AS colid,
                               generate_series(1, array_length(c.conkey, 1)) AS arridx
                    ) AS cols
                    JOIN pg_attribute AS ca ON cols.colid = ca.attnum
                    WHERE ca.attrelid = c.conrelid
                    ORDER BY cols.arridx
                ),
                c.contype,
                (SELECT fkc.relname || '.' || fka.attname
                FROM pg_attribute AS fka
                JOIN pg_class AS fkc ON fka.attrelid = fkc.oid
                WHERE fka.attrelid = c.confrelid AND fka.attnum = c.confkey[1]),
                cl.reloptions
            FROM pg_constraint AS c
            JOIN pg_class AS cl ON c.conrelid = cl.oid
            JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON cl.relnamespace = ns.oid
            WHERE ns.nspname = 'public' AND cl.relname = 'social_auth_usersocialauth'
        ; args=['public', 'social_auth_usersocialauth']
[2017-12-13 23:35:00] DEBUG [django.db.backends:111] (0.120) 
            SELECT
                indexname, array_agg(attname ORDER BY rnum), indisunique, indisprimary,
                array_agg(ordering ORDER BY rnum), amname, exprdef, s2.attoptions
            FROM (
                SELECT
                    row_number() OVER () as rnum, c2.relname as indexname,
                    idx.*, attr.attname, am.amname,
                    CASE
                        WHEN idx.indexprs IS NOT NULL THEN
                            pg_get_indexdef(idx.indexrelid)
                    END AS exprdef,
                    CASE am.amname
                        WHEN 'btree' THEN
                            CASE (option & 1)
                                WHEN 1 THEN 'DESC' ELSE 'ASC'
                            END
                    END as ordering,
                    c2.reloptions as attoptions
                FROM (
                    SELECT
                        *, unnest(i.indkey) as key, unnest(i.indoption) as option
                    FROM pg_index i
                ) idx
                LEFT JOIN pg_class c ON idx.indrelid = c.oid
                LEFT JOIN pg_class c2 ON idx.indexrelid = c2.oid
                LEFT JOIN pg_am am ON c2.relam = am.oid
                LEFT JOIN pg_attribute attr ON attr.attrelid = c.oid AND attr.attnum = idx.key
                WHERE c.relname = 'social_auth_usersocialauth'
            ) s2
            GROUP BY indexname, indisunique, indisprimary, amname, exprdef, attoptions;
        ; args=['social_auth_usersocialauth']
